<Response>None</Response><Text>If you're looking for a new nail salon, this is the place you want. The ladies there do amazing work and are super fun to be around. Without being overly chatty, they're friendly and funny. I tried several different services there. It's obvious why they have so many loyal customers.

Nails: I didn't get my nails done, but I watched them work as I got my pedicure. Absolutely beautiful!

Pedicure: While I did miss the massage chairs at my old place, the amazing "mud" they used made up for it. I chose the milk (for dry skin) instead of the lavender mud. I am in love! I'm not used to soaking my feet in a bucket instead of a foot tub thing, but it was so cool. It was hard to sit still because my toes kept wanting to play with mud. They also had an insane variety of nail colors to choose from. The man also worked extra long on my very callused feet for no extra charge. They're so nice and soft/smooth now!

Brow wax: Fast and good. The only complaint I have is that the bits she missed with the wax were trimmed instead of plucked.

Leg wax: This wasn't on their list of services but they do it. I had a mixed experience with this one. She uses a wax that hardens and peels off (because it is gentler on the skin, causes less bumpiness, and doesn't leave the skin all sticky afterwards) but it didn't work for me. It could be because my skin is ridiculously dry, but it was pretty miserable as she slowly yanked bits of wax free. To be fair,  she said this usually doesn't happen. After probably 20-30 minutes of torture, she switched to the old style wax and it was quick and a LOT less painful. Next time, I'll ask for that kind from the start. I want to be clear, that woman tried amazingly hard to give me a great leg wax, and she delivered. I would have given up and switched waxes earlier, but she was determined to make it work for me because she knew I'd love the results.< /Text><date>1510266429100<//date><gmap_id>0x8085143644aab8e1:0x690dd67147293f44</gmap_id>< user_name>
Laura Watkins (House of Geekiness)</user_name>

<text>Can you say, "Sanitary!"? This place uses individual deep baskets lined with disposable bags. Every kit is in a closed and processed autoclave bag. All sand files, sponges, buffers are tiny ones that are thrown away after your pedi. They put the foot scrub into tiny disposable "sauce-type" lidded containers so no "double-dipping" into a huge communal jar of scrub. All other products are dispensed out squirt bottles. The techs are gentle and do not aggressively go after or injure the sides of your big toe. Your feet NEVER touch anything that could hide germs or fungus! Brought Hubby for his first pedi. He loved it! We got the Crystal Mud pedi and my feet feel so soft and hydrated. Love this place & I'm coming back!< /text><Pictures>None</Pictures><Response>None< /Response>< Gmap_id>

<text>2/2/15

The first thing I noticed when I walked into this Jamba Juice was how clean it was. It was 7 p.m. so perhaps the rush of daytime crowds had long passed - but still it was a couple hours before closing. The two guys working tonight were cleaning up but stopped to greet and help me. I was meeting a friend who had showed up first - I sat down at a (clean!) table with her and her boyfriend to look over some papers and happily reminisced about once upon a time sixteen years ago when I was the seventeen year old behind that juice counter.

I talked for a minute with Josh and Thomas before I left - they were really friendly employees. No music playing (perhaps there's a manager somewhere reading these reviews), and they actually seemed happy to be at work. I enjoyed my visit in here much more than the last time I was inside a Jamba Juice, and I left with a smile on my face!<//text>< Gmap_id>

< Text>
BMW M4 saved by ABC Auto Care after lazy diagnosis from BMW dealership!

First off, 100% recommendation. Easily the best service I've received when it comes to diagnosis/repairs. Upfront, honest and will find the root cause of the issue.

I have a 2015 BMW M4 that had a rough idle and low coolant. Originally I brought it into a BMW dealership in Camarillo. They ran a vacuum leak test and they said it was all good (it was not all good...coolant was low, obvious leak somewhere) After questioning and paying the BMW dealership a crazy amount of money for nothing I brought my vehicle to ABC auto care for a second opinion.

They diagnosed deeper than the initial vacuum test, and found an internal leak in the intercooler. This is a huge issue, but difficult to notice for an average dude like me. No check engine light, just a rougher idle then normal and physically low coolant in top intercooler tank. If I waited longer and trusted the BMW dealership diagnosis, my engine would be toast.

Anders from ABC Auto Care made sure everything was taken care of, great communication and up front about the severity of the issue (including pictures and price quotes before moving forward on installs/labor). If I got this work done at the dealership, it would have been a 5k+ ordeal easily. ABC saved me a ton of money in this category. Loaner car for free (first come first serve). Took less then a week to obtain parts, clean, install etc. To top it all off Anders went out of his way to find an extended warranty that pertains to this issue, potentially saving me more money.

My M4 now runs like the day I bought it, smooth and back to normal power. If you are contemplating bringing a higher end car in, have zero worries. A+++ in all categories</Text>

<Text>Either the mechanic tried to scam me, or doesn't know anything about rear differentials.

My wife's explorer had a metallic grinding sound coming from the back tire. We took her car to ABC Auto Care, where they said that the entire rear differential needed to be replaced, for just under $3k.

I am by no means an auto expert, but knew that my wife's car had independent rear suspension, so if there is a problem on one side, they only need to do work on the problem side, not both. Their quote for only working the problem side was $400 less.

I didn't feel comfortable with the quote, so I took the car somewhere else for a second opinion (Coastal Differential Repair). Turns out, the sound was because the lining of the emergency brake on the right side had worn completely off, and the spring had broken off into the rotor, which was causing the sound. I asked the mechanic if there was anything wrong with the rear differential, he said it just needed to be serviced. He did everything for under $320.

So, not only would ABC Auto Care have done unnecessary work, but they also wouldn't have fixed the actual problem. At least they only cost me $70 for a "diagnostic fee."

Update: I did have a good talk with the owner. He refunded my $70 for diagnostic fee, and seems genuinely upset at my experience.< /Text><Rate>1<//Rate>< Gmap_id>

First, let me say that booking the appointment was fast and easy.  On the day of the appointment, the dispatcher told me that the cleaning team could come an hour earlier, so that was a nice bonus. When the team go tthere, the lead took a quick walk-through and determined that the 3-hour estimate was not enough. She called HQ, and HQ asked me if an additional hour was acceptable. It was. It was great that they checked with me for advance approval, instead of getting 2/3 the way through and then asking. That's a good business practice. I appreciated it.

The cleaners did a fantastic job. They cleaned a lot of places I never thought of and did not expect them to clean. (above doorway moldings, the outsides of windows, the tracks for sliding windows).  When they were done, the place looked brand new. The team leader took time to show me some places that they were not able to clean because of access or misfunctioning sliding doors. I appreciated the candor.

Pricing was fair, even though they had to add one hour to the estimate.  I strongly recommend Green USA Cleaning.</review>
